[Command Aliases](#command-aliases)\n2. [Tab Autocomplete](#tab-autocomplete)\n3. [Command Chaining](#command-chaining)\n4. [Command Scripts](#command-scripts)\n5. [Command Scheduling](#command-scheduling)\n6. [Command History](#command-history)\n7. [Risk Levels](#risk-levels)\n\n---\n\n## Command Aliases\n\nQuick shortcuts for common commands.\n\n### Single-Character Aliases\n```\nh     → /help\ns     → /status\ni     → /initialize\nc     → /clear\n```\n\n### Multi-Word Aliases\n```\nls, sl     → /state list\nse         → /state evolve\nsr         → /state regenerate\nsrb        → /state rollback\noa         → /org agents\noc         → /org chart\nll         → /llm status\n```\n\n### Module Shortcuts\n```\nswarm      → /swarm status\ngate       → /gate list\ndomain     → /domain list\nconstraint → /constraint list\nartifact   → /artifact list\ndoc        → /document create\nverify     → /verify content\n```\n\n### Managing Custom Aliases\n```bash\n/alias list                    # Show all aliases\n/alias create <name> <cmd>     # Create custom alias\n/alias delete <name>           # Delete custom alias\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```bash\n/alias create check /status /llm status\ncheck                           # Runs both commands\n```\n\n---\n\n## Tab Autocomplete\n\nPress **Tab** to autocomplete commands or see suggestions.\n\n### Usage\n1. Type partial command: `/sta`\n2. Press **Tab**\n3. See suggestions or autocomplete\n\n### Examples\n```bash\n/s<TAB>          # Shows: status, state list, script list, swarm status\n/st<TAB>         # Autocompletes to: /state \n/state l<TAB>    # Autocompletes to: /state list \n/org a<TAB>      # Autocompletes to: /org agents \n```\n\n### Suggestion Display\n- ✓ Green check = Command is implemented\n- ○ Orange circle = Command is planned\n- Shows module name and description\n- Click to select\n\n---\n\n## Command Chaining\n\nUse `|` to chain multiple commands together.\n\n### Basic Usage\n```bash\n/command1 | /command2 | /command3\n```\n\n### Examples\n```bash\n# Initialize and check status\n/initialize | /status\n\n# List states then evolve first one\n/state list | /state evolve 1\n\n# Full workflow chain\n/initialize | /state list | /org agents | /status\n\n# Get status and then list agents\n/status | /org agents\n```\n\n### Chain Behavior\n- Commands execute left to right\n- Output from command N becomes input to command N+1\n- Chain stops on error\n- Shows visual markers: ├─ and └─\n\n---\n\n## Command Scripts\n\nExecute multiple commands with a single script.\n\n### Built-in Scripts\n```bash\n/init-and-explore    → Initialize, status, states, agents\n/full-workflow       → Initialize, states, evolve, gates\n/agent-check         → Check agents, LLMs, system status\n```\n\n### Script Commands\n```bash\n/script list                          # List all scripts\n/script run <name>                    # Run a script\n/script create <name> <cmd1> <cmd2>   # Create custom script\n/script delete <name>                 # Delete script\n```\n\n### Examples\n```bash\n# List available scripts\n/script list\n\n# Run built-in script\n/script run init-and-explore\n\n# Create custom script\n/script create my-routine /status /state list /org agents\n\n# Run custom script\n/script run my-routine\n\n# Delete script\n/script delete my-routine\n```\n\n### Script Workflow\nScripts execute commands sequentially:\n- Each command completes before next starts\n- Script stops on error\n- Shows progress for each command\n\n---\n\n## Command Scheduling\n\nSchedule commands to run at specific times.\n\n### Schedule Commands\n```bash\n/schedule list                     # List scheduled commands\n/schedule add <HH:MM> <command>    # Schedule a command\n/schedule remove <id>              # Remove scheduled command\n```\n\n### Examples\n```bash\n# Schedule status check for 10:00 AM\n/schedule add 10:00 /status\n\n# Schedule state evolution for 2:30 PM\n/schedule add 14:30 /state evolve 1\n\n# Schedule multiple commands\n/schedule add 09:00 /initialize\n/schedule add 09:15 /status\n/schedule add 09:30 /org agents\n\n# View scheduled commands\n/schedule list\n\n# Remove a scheduled command\n/schedule remove 1234567890\n```\n\n### Time Format\n- 24-hour format: HH:MM\n- Example: 10:00, 14:30, 23:45\n- If time has passed today, schedules for tomorrow\n\n### Scheduler Behavior\n- Checks every second\n- Executes command at scheduled time\n- Must have tab open to execute\n- Stores result (completed/failed)\n\n---\n\n## Command History\n\nView your command execution history.\n\n### History Commands\n```bash\n/history           # View command history\n/history clear     # Clear command history\n```\n\n### History Features\n- Shows last 1000 commands\n- Includes timestamp\n- Shows success/failure\n- Shows risk level\n- Persists across sessions\n\n### Example Output\n```\nCommand history:\n  1. /status\n  2. /state list\n  3. /state evolve 1\n  4. /initialize | /status\n```\n\n### Arrow Keys\n- **Arrow Up** - Navigate back in history\n- **Arrow Down** - Navigate forward in history\n\n---\n\n## Risk Levels\n\nCommands are classified by risk level.\n\n### LOW Risk\nExecutes immediately, no confirmation.\n```\nhelp, status, initialize, clear\nstate list, org agents, org chart\nllm status, gate list, domain list\nconstraint list, artifact list\n```\n\n### MEDIUM Risk\nShows risk level, may require confirmation.\n```\nstate evolve, state regenerate\nswarm create, gate validate\ndomain analyze, constraint add\ndocument magnify, document simplify\n```\n\n### HIGH Risk\nRequires confirmation before execution.\n```\nstate rollback, org assign\nswarm execute, gate create\ndomain create, document solidify\nartifact delete\n```\n\n### Risk Colors\n- 🟢 GREEN = LOW\n- 🟡 YELLOW = MEDIUM\n- 🔴 RED = HIGH\n\n### Example\n```bash\n/status                  # LOW - executes immediately\n/state evolve 1          # MEDIUM - shows risk level\n/state rollback 1        # HIGH - requires confirmation\n```\n\n---\n\n## Advanced Examples\n\n### Example 1: Morning Routine Script\n```bash\n/script create morning-routine /initialize /status /org agents /llm status\n/script run morning-routine\n```\n\n### Example 2: Scheduled Daily Checks\n```bash\n/schedule add 09:00 /status\n/schedule add 12:00 /state list\n/schedule add 18:00 /org agents\n```\n\n### Example 3: Custom Alias for Common Task\n```bash\n/alias create check-all /status /llm status /org agents\ncheck-all\n```\n\n### Example 4: Complex Chain\n```bash\n/initialize | /state list | /state evolve 1 | /gate list | /status\n```\n\n### Example 5: Using History\n```bash\n# View recent commands\n/history\n\n# Use arrow keys to navigate\n# Press Enter to re-execute\n```\n\n---\n\n## Tips & Tricks\n\n1. **Use aliases for frequently used commands**\n   ```bash\n   # Instead of typing /state list every time\n   /alias create sl /state list\n   sl  # Much faster!\n   ```\n\n2. **Chain commands for workflows**\n   ```bash\n   # One command instead of four\n   /init | /status | /state list | /org agents\n   ```\n\n3. **Create scripts for repetitive tasks**\n   ```bash\n   # Save time with scripts\n   /script create daily /status /state list /org agents\n   /script run daily\n   ```\n\n4. **Schedule maintenance tasks**\n   ```bash\n   # Automate regular checks\n   /schedule add 10:00 /status\n   /schedule add 14:00 /llm status\n   ```\n\n5. **Use Tab to explore commands**\n   ```bash\n   # Don\'t remember exact command?\n   /sw<TAB>  # See all swarm commands\n   ```\n\n6. **Check risk before executing**\n   ```bash\n   # Unsure about a command?\n   # Try it with low-risk first\n   /state list     # LOW - safe to try\n   /state evolve   # MEDIUM - shows risk\n   /state rollback # HIGH - be careful!\n   ```\n\n7. **Review history to audit actions**\n   ```bash\n   /history  # See what you\'ve done\n   ```\n\n---\n\n## Keyboard Shortcuts\n\n| Key | Action |\n|-----|--------|\n| Enter | Execute command |\n| Tab | Autocomplete |\n| Arrow Up | Previous command in history |\n| Arrow Down | Next command in history |\n| Escape | Clear suggestions |\n\n---\n\n## Storage & Persistence\n\nAll enhancements use **localStorage** for persistence:\n\n- **Custom aliases**: Survive page refresh\n- **Command history**: Survive page refresh (1000 entries)\n- **Custom scripts**: Survive page refresh\n- **Scheduled commands**: Survive page refresh\n\n**Note:** localStorage is browser-specific. Data doesn\'t sync across browsers or devices.\n\n---\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Autocomplete not working?\n- Make sure terminal input is focused\n- Press Tab after typing partial command\n- Check browser console for errors\n\n### Custom alias not working?\n- Check alias was created: `/alias list`\n- Verify alias name is correct\n- Try recreating: `/alias create <name> <command>`\n\n### Script not executing?\n- Check script exists: `/script list`\n- Verify script name is correct\n- Check terminal for error messages\n\n### Scheduled command didn\'t run?\n- Verify time format (HH:MM)\n- Check if tab was open at scheduled time\n- Review scheduled commands: `/schedule list`\n- Check terminal for errors\n\n### Command chain stops early?\n- Review terminal output for errors\n- Check each command in the chain\n- Test commands individually first\n\n---\n\n## Need More Help?\n\nType `/help` in the terminal to see all available commands.\n\nFor detailed documentation, see:\n- `PRIORITY3_IMPLEMENTATION_COMPLETE.md` - Full implementation details\n- `priority3_plan.md` - Implementation plan\n- `MURPHY_SYSTEM_MASTER_SPECIFICATION.md` - Master system specification\n\n---\n\n**Version:** Murphy System v2.0  \n**Priority 3 Status:** ✅ Complete  \n**Date:** January 21, 2026\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

logging\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\nclass LLMProvider(Enum):\n    """Available LLM providers"""\n    GROQ = "groq"\n    ARISTOTLE = "aristotle"\n    ONBOARD = "onboard"\n\n\nclass LLMResponseQuality(Enum):\n    """Response quality levels"""\n    EXCELLENT = "excellent"\n    GOOD = "good"\n    ACCEPTABLE = "acceptable"\n    POOR = "poor"\n    INVALID = "invalid"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass LLMResponse:\n    """LLM response data structure"""\n    content: str\n    provider: LLMProvider\n    model: str\n    tokens_used: int\n    confidence: float\n    quality: LLMResponseQuality\n    cached: bool\n    generation_time: float\n    timestamp: datetime\n    \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:\n        """Convert to dictionary"""\n        return {\n            \'content\': self.content,\n            \'provider\': self.provider.value,\n            \'model\': self.model,\n            \'tokens_used\': self.tokens_used,\n            \'confidence\': self.confidence,\n            \'quality\': self.quality.value,\n            \'cached\': self.cached,\n            \'generation_time\': self.generation_time,\n            \'timestamp\': self.timestamp.isoformat()\n        }\n\n\nclass RateLimiter:\n    """Rate limiter for API calls"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, max_calls: int = 60, time_window: int = 60):\n        """\n        Initialize rate limiter\n        \n        Args:\n            max_calls: Maximum number of calls allowed\n            time_window: Time window in seconds\n        """\n        self.max_calls = max_calls\n        self.time_window = time_window\n        self.calls = []\n        self.lock = asyncio.Lock()\n    \n    async def acquire(self) -> bool:\n        """\n        Acquire permission to make a call\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if call is allowed, False otherwise\n        """\n        async with self.lock:\n            now = time.time()\n            # Remove calls outside the time window\n            self.calls = [call_time for call_time in self.calls \n                         if now - call_time < self.time_window]\n            \n            if len(self.calls) < self.max_calls:\n                self.calls.append(now)\n                return True\n            \n            # Calculate wait time\n            oldest_call = self.calls[0]\n            wait_time = self.time_window - (now - oldest_call)\n            logger.warning(f"Rate limit reached. Wait {wait_time:.2f} seconds")\n            return False\n    \n    async def wait_for_slot(self, timeout: int = 30) -> bool:\n        """\n        Wait for an available slot\n        \n        Args:\n            timeout: Maximum time to wait in seconds\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if slot acquired, False if timeout\n        """\n        start_time = time.time()\n        while time.time() - start_time < timeout:\n            if await self.acquire():\n                return True\n            await asyncio.sleep(1)\n        return False\n\n\nclass ResponseCache:\n    """Cache for LLM responses"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, ttl: int = 3600):\n        """\n        Initialize cache\n        \n        Args:\n            ttl: Time to live for cache entries in seconds\n        """\n        self.cache: Dict[str, Tuple[LLMResponse, datetime]] = {}\n        self.ttl = ttl\n        self.lock = asyncio.Lock()\n    \n    def _generate_key(self, prompt: str, model: str, **kwargs) -> str:\n        """Generate cache key"""\n        key_data = {\n            \'prompt\': prompt,\n            \'model\': model,\n            **kwargs\n        }\n        key_str = json.dumps(key_data, sort_keys=True)\n        return hashlib.sha256(key_str.encode()).hexdigest()\n    \n    async def get(self, prompt: str, model: str, **kwargs) -> Optional[LLMResponse]:\n        """\n        Get cached response\n        \n        Args:\n            prompt: The prompt\n            model: The model name\n            **kwargs: Additional parameters\n        \n        Returns:\n            Cached response or None\n        """\n        async with self.lock:\n            key = self._generate_key(prompt, model, **kwargs)\n            \n            if key not in self.cache:\n                return None\n            \n            response, cached_at = self.cache[key]\n            \n            # Check if expired\n            if datetime.now() - cached_at > timedelta(seconds=self.ttl):\n                del self.cache[key]\n                return None\n            \n            logger.info(f"Cache hit for key: {key[:16]}...")\n            response.cached = True\n            return response\n    \n    async def set(self, prompt: str, model: str, response: LLMResponse, **kwargs):\n        """\n        Cache a response\n        \n        Args:\n            prompt: The prompt\n            model: The model name\n            response: The response to cache\n            **kwargs: Additional parameters\n        """\n        async with self.lock:\n            key = self._generate_key(prompt, model, **kwargs)\n            self.cache[key] = (response, datetime.now())\n            logger.info(f"Cached response for key: {key[:16]}...")\n    \n    async def clear(self):\n        """Clear all cache entries"""\n        async with self.lock:\n            self.cache.clear()\n            logger.info("Cache cleared")\n    \n    async def cleanup_expired(self):\n        """Remove expired cache entries"""\n        async with self.lock:\n            now = datetime.now()\n            expired_keys = [\n                key for key, (_, cached_at) in self.cache.items()\n                if now - cached_at > timedelta(seconds=self.ttl)\n            ]\n            \n            for key in expired_keys:\n                del self.cache[key]\n            \n            if expired_keys:\n                logger.info(f"Cleaned up {len(expired_keys)} expired cache entries")\n\n\nclass LLMClientManager:\n    """Manager for LLM API clients"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        """Initialize LLM client manager"""\n        self.providers: Dict[LLMProvider, Any] = {}\n        self.rate_limiters: Dict[LLMProvider, 0,\n            \'provider_calls\': {provider.value: 0 for provider in LLMProvider},\n            \'errors\': 0,\n            \'retries\': 0\n        }\n        \n        self._initialize_providers()\n    \n    def _initialize_providers(self):\n        """Initialize LLM providers"""\n        # Groq API\n        groq_keys = [\n            \'gsk_VKqX3lfpHlXpQz5JZpXpQz5JZpXpQz5JZpXpQz5JZpXpQz5J\',\n            \'gsk_VKqX3lfpHlXpQz5JZpXpQz5JZpXpQz5JZpXpQz5JZpXpQz5J\',\n            # Add remaining 7 keys...\n        ]\n        \n        # Filter out placeholder keys\n        groq_keys = [key for key in groq_keys if not key.startswith(\'gsk_VKqX3lfp\')]\n        \n        if groq_keys:\n            from groq_client import GroqClient\n            self.providers[LLMProvider.GROQ] = GroqClient(\n                api_keys=groq_keys,\n                model=\'mixtral-8x7b-32768\',\n                temperature=0.7\n            )\n            self.rate_limiters[LLMProvider.GROQ] = RateLimiter(\n                max_calls=60, time_window=60\n            )\n            logger.info(f"Initialized Groq with {len(groq_keys)} API keys")\n        \n        # Aristotle API\n        aristotle_key = \'arstl_D7uKG0m-c3fs_4pRRBZ9wxnYGDVVLgTCLIKkH0UD2vQ\'\n        \n        if aristotle_key:\n            from aristotle_client import (fallback)")\n    \n    async def call_llm(\n        self,\n        prompt: str,\n        provider: Optional[LLMProvider] = None,\n        model: Optional[str] = None,\n        temperature: Optional[float] = None,\n        max_tokens: int = 2048,\n        use_cache: bool = True,\n        retries: int = 3,\n        **kwargs\n    ) -> LLMResponse:\n        """\n        Call LLM with automatic retry and fallback\n        \n        Args:\n            prompt: The prompt to send\n            provider: Preferred provider (None for automatic selection)\n            model: Model name (None for provider default)\n            temperature: Temperature (None for provider default)\n            max_tokens: Maximum tokens\n            use_cache: Whether to use cache\n            retries: Number of retry attempts\n            **kwargs: Additional parameters\n        \n        Returns:\n            LLMResponse object\n        """\n        self.call_stats[\'total_calls\'] += 1\n        \n        # Try cache first\n        if use_cache:\n            cached = await self.cache.get(prompt, model or \'default\', **kwargs)\n            if cached:\n                self.call_stats[\'cache_hits\'] += 1\n                return cached\n            else:\n                self.call_stats[\'cache_misses\'] += 1\n        \n        # Determine provider preference order\n        provider_order = self._get_provider_order(provider)\n        \n        # Try each provider in order\n        last_error = None\n        for attempt in range(retries):\n            for current_provider in provider_order:\n                try:\n                    # Check rate limit\n                    rate_limiter = self.rate_limiters.get(current_provider)\n                    if rate_limiter:\n                        if not await rate_limiter.wait_for_slot():\n                            logger.warning(f"Rate limit reached for {current_provider.value}")\n                            continue\n                    \n                    # Get client\n                    client = self.providers.get(current_provider)\n                    if not client:\n                        continue\n                    \n                    # Make API call\n                    start_time = time.time()\n                    content, tokens_used = await client.generate(\n                        prompt=prompt,\n                        model=model,\n                        temperature=temperature,\n                        max_tokens=max_tokens,\n                        **kwargs\n                    )\n                    generation_time = time.time() - start_time\n                    \n                    # Validate response\n                    if not self._validate_response(content):\n                        raise ValueError("Invalid response from LLM")\n                    \n                    # Create response object\n                    response = LLMResponse(\n                        content=content,\n                        provider=current_provider,\n                        model=model or client.model,\n                        tokens_used=tokens_used,\n                        confidence=self._calculate_confidence(content),\n                        quality=self._assess_quality(content),\n                        cached=False,\n                        generation_time=generation_time,\n                        timestamp=datetime.now()\n                    )\n                    \n                    # Cache response\n                    if use_cache:\n                        await self.cache.set(prompt, model or \'default\', response, **kwargs)\n                    \n                    # Update stats\n                    self.call_stats[\'provider_calls\'][current_provider.value] += 1\n                    \n                    logger.info(f"LLM call successful: {current_provider.value}, "\n                               f"tokens={tokens_used}, time={generation_time:.2f}s")\n                    \n                    return response\n                \n                except Exception as e:\n                    last_error = e\n                    self.call_stats[\'errors\'] += 1\n                    logger.error(f"LLM call failed: {current_provider.value}, "\n                               f"attempt {attempt + 1}/{retries}, error: {str(e)}")\n                    \n                    # Retry with exponential backoff\n                    if attempt < retries - 1:\n                        backoff_time = (2 ** attempt) * 1.0\n                        await asyncio.sleep(backoff_time)\n                        self.call_stats[\'retries\'] += 1\n                    else:\n                        logger.error(f"All retry attempts failed for {current_provider.value}")\n        \n        # All providers failed\n        logger.error(f"All LLM providers failed. Last error: {str(last_error)}")\n        raise RuntimeError(f"Failed to get LLM response: {str(last_error)}")\n    \n    def _get_provider_order(self, preferred: Optional[LLMProvider]) -> List[LLMProvider]:\n        """Get provider preference order"""\n        if preferred:\n            return [preferred] + [p for p in LLMProvider if p != preferred]\n        return [LLMProvider.GROQ, LLMProvider.ARISTOTLE, LLMProvider.ONBOARD]\n    \n    def _validate_response(self, content: str) -> bool:\n        """Validate LLM response"""\n        if not content or len(content.strip()) < 10:\n            return False\n        return True\n    \n    def _calculate_confidence(self, content: str) -> float:\n        """Calculate confidence score for response"""\n        # Simple heuristic based on content length and structure\n        confidence = 0.5\n        \n        # Length factor\n        if len(content) > 100:\n            confidence += 0.2\n        if len(content) > 500:\n            confidence += 0.1\n        \n        # Structure factor (has paragraphs, lists, etc.)\n        if \'\\n\' in content:\n            confidence += 0.1\n        if any(marker in content for marker in [\'•\', \'-\', \'1.\', \'2.\', \'3.\']):\n            confidence += 0.1\n        \n        return min(confidence, 1.0)\n    \n    def _assess_quality(self, content: str) -> LLMResponseQuality:\n        """Assess response quality"""\n        confidence = self._calculate_confidence(content)\n        \n        if confidence >= 0.9:\n            return LLMResponseQuality.EXCELLENT\n        elif confidence >= 0.7:\n            return LLMResponseQuality.GOOD\n        elif confidence >= 0.5:\n            return LLMResponseQuality.ACCEPTABLE\n        elif confidence >= 0.3:\n            return LLMResponseQuality.POOR\n        else:\n            return LLMResponseQuality.INVALID\n    \n    def get_stats(self) -> Dict:\n        """Get call statistics"""\n        return self.call_stats.copy()\n    \n    async def clear_cache(self):\n        """Clear response cache"""\n        await self.cache.clear()\n    \n    async def cleanup_cache(self):\n        """Clean up expired cache entries"""\n        await self.cache.cleanup_expired()\n\n\n# Global instance\nllm_manager = LLMClientManager()\n\n\nasync def test_llm_integration():\n    """Test LLM integration"""\n    print("Testing LLM Integration...")\n    \n    # {'role': 'assistant', 'content': 'Now let me create the response validator to ensure LLM responses meet quality standards.\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="response_validator.py">\n"""\nMurphy System - LLM Response Validator\nEnsures responses meet quality and safety standards\n"""\n\nimport re\nimport logging\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Tuple\nfrom enum import Enum\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\nclass ValidationResult(Enum):\n    """Validation result types"""\n    VALID = "valid"\n    WARNING = "warning"\n    INVALID = "invalid"\n\n\nclass ResponseValidator:\n    """Validates LLM responses"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        """Initialize validator"""\n        self.min_length = 20\n        self.max_length = 10000\n        self.prohibited_patterns = [\n            r\'<script[^>]*>.*?</script>\',  # Scripts\n            r\'javascript:\',  # JavaScript URLs\n            r\'data:text/html\',  # Data URLs\n            r\'eval\\s*\\(\',  # eval() calls\n        ]\n        self.required_structure_indicators = [\n            r\'[.!?]\',  # Sentence endings\n            r\'\\n\',  # Line breaks\n        ]\n    \n    def validate(self, content: str) -> Tuple[ValidationResult, Dict]:\n        """\n        Validate LLM response\n        \n        Args:\n            content: Response content to validate\n        \n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (result, validation_details)\n        """\n        validation_details = {\n            \'length_valid\': False,\n            \'no_prohibited_content\': False,\n            \'has_structure\': False,\n            \'is_meaningful\': False,\n            \'issues\': [],\n            \'warnings\': []\n        }\n        \n        # Check length\n        length_valid = self._check_length(content)\n        validation_details[\'length_valid\'] = length_valid\n        if not length_valid:\n            validation_details[\'issues\'].append("Response too short or too long")\n        \n        # Check for prohibited content\n        no_prohibited = self._check_prohibited_content(content)\n        validation_details[\'no_prohibited_content\'] = no_prohibited\n        if not no_prohibited:\n            validation_details[\'issues\'].append("Contains prohibited content")\n        \n        # Check structure\n        has_structure = self._check_structure(content)\n        validation_details[\'has_structure\'] = has_structure\n        if not has_structure:\n            validation_details[\'warnings\'].append("Response lacks proper structure")\n        \n        # Check if meaningful\n        is_meaningful = self._check_meaningful(content)\n        validation_details[\'is_meaningful\'] = is_meaningful\n        if not is_meaningful:\n            validation_details[\'issues\'].append("Response is not meaningful")\n        \n        # Determine overall result\n        if validation_details[\'issues\']:\n            result = ValidationResult.INVALID\n        elif validation_details[\'warnings\']:\n            result = ValidationResult.WARNING\n        else:\n            result = ValidationResult.VALID\n        \n        return result, validation_details\n    \n    def _check_length(self, content: str) -> bool:\n        """Check content length"""\n        length = len(content.strip())\n        return self.min_length <= length <= self.max_length\n    \n    def _check_prohibited_content(self, content: str) -> bool:\n        """Check for prohibited content patterns"""\n        for pattern in self.prohibited_patterns:\n            if re.search(pattern, content, re.IGNORECASE | re.DOTALL):\n                logger.warning(f"Prohibited pattern found: {pattern}")\n                return False\n        return True\n    \n    def _check_structure(self, content: str) -> bool:\n        """Check if content has proper structure"""\n        for indicator in self.required_structure_indicators:\n            if re.search(indicator, content):\n                return True\n        return False\n    \n    def _check_meaningful(self, content: str) -> bool:\n        """Check if content is meaningful"""\n        # Check for minimum word count\n        words = content.strip().split()\n        if len(words) < 5:\n            return False\n        \n        # Check for repetitive content\n        unique_words = set(words)\n        if len(unique_words) / len(words) < 0.3:\n            logger.warning("Response has too much repetition")\n            return False\n        \n        # Check for coherent sentences\n        sentences = re.split(r\'[.!?]+\', content)\n        meaningful_sentences = [s for s in sentences if len(s.strip()) > 10]\n        if len(meaningful_sentences) < 1:\n            return False\n        \n        return True\n    \n    def validate_json(self, content: str) -> Tuple[bool, Dict]:\n        """\n        Validate JSON content\n        \n        Args:\n            content: JSON string to validate\n        \n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (is_valid, parsed_json_or_error)\n        """\n        import json\n        \n        try:\n            parsed = json.loads(content)\n            return True, parsed\n        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:\n            error_msg = f"Invalid JSON: {str(e)}"\n            logger.error(error_msg)\n            return False, {\'error\': error_msg}\n    \n    def validate_code(self, content: str, language: str = None) -> Tuple[bool, str]:\n        """\n        Validate code content\n        \n        Args:\n            content: Code to validate\n            language: Programming language\n        \n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (is_valid, error_message)\n        """\n        # Basic checks\n        if not content or len(content.strip()) < 10:\n            return False, "Code is too short"\n        \n        # Check for common code patterns\n        code_indicators = [\n            r\'function\\s+\\w+\\s*\\(\',  # Function definition\n            r\'class\\s+\\w+\',  # Class definition\n            r\'import\\s+\\w+\',  # Import statement\n            r\'def\\s+\\w+\\s*\\(\',  # Python function\n            r\'if\\s*\\(\',  # If statement\n            r\'return\\s+\',  # Return statement\n        ]\n        \n        has_code = any(re.search(pattern, content) for pattern in code_indicators)\n        \n        if not has_code:\n            return False, "Content does not appear to be valid code"\n        \n        return True, ""\n    \n    def sanitize(self, content: str) -> str:\n        """\n        Sanitize content by removing or escaping dangerous elements\n        \n        Args:\n            content: Content to sanitize\n        \n        Returns:\n            Sanitized content\n        """\n        sanitized = content\n        \n        # Test rate limit\n        acquired = await limiter.acquire()\n        if not acquired:\n            print("✓ Rate limit enforced correctly")\n        else:\n            print("✗ Rate limit not enforced")\n            return False\n        \n        #   - Clear terminal\n\nState Commands:\n  /state list             - List all states\n  /state evolve <id>      - Evolve a state\n  /state regenerate <id>  - Regenerate a state\n  /state rollback <id>    - Rollback a state\n\nOrganization Commands:\n  /org agents             - List all agents\n  /org chart              - Show organization chart\n\nLLM Commands:\n  /llm status             - Show LLM status\n  /llm generate <prompt>  - Generate text with LLM\n  /llm verify <content>   - Verify with Aristotle\n"""\n    \n    return """\nMurphy System v2.0 - Command Help\n\nCore Commands:\n  /help [topic]           - Show help information\n  /status                 - Show system status\n  /initialize             - Initialize the system\n  /clear                  - Clear terminal\n\nState       - View command history\n  /script [list|run|create|delete] - Manage scripts\n  /schedule [list|add|remove] - Schedule commands\n\nUse Tab for autocomplete, Arrow keys for history.\n"""\n\n\ndef get_basic_status():\n    """Get basic status text"""\n    return f"""\nMurphy System Status\n\nSystem ID: {system_state[\'system_id\']}\nInitialized: {system_state[\'initialized\']}\nLLM Enabled: {system_state[\'llm_stats\'][\'state_calls\']}\n  Total Enhancements: {system_state[\'llm_stats\'][\'total_llm_enhancements\']}\n"""\n\n\ndef get_basic_state_info(state_id, action):\n    """Get basic state information"""\n    state = system_state[\'states\'].get(state_id)\n    \n    if not state:\n        return f"State {state_id} not found"\n    \n    return f"""\nState {action}: initialized")\n    \n    def get_risk_level(self, operation: OperationType) -> RiskLevel:\n        """\n        Get risk level for operation\n        \n        Args:\n            operation: Operation type\n        \n        Returns:\n            Risk level\n        """\n        if operation in self.high_risk_operations:\n            return RiskLevel.HIGH\n        elif operation in self.medium_risk_operations:\n            return RiskLevel.MEDIUM\n        else:\n            return RiskLevel.LOW\n    \n    def requires_verification(self, operation: OperationType) -> bool:\n        """\n        Check if operation requires verification\n        \n        Args:\n            operation: Operation type\n        \n        Returns:\n            True if verification required\n        """\n        risk_level = self.get_risk_level(operation)\n        return risk_level in [RiskLevel.MEDIUM, RiskLevel.HIGH, RiskLevel.CRITICAL]\n    \n    async def verify_operation(\n        self,\n        operation: OperationType,\n        content: str,\n        context: Dict = None,\n        custom_criteria: str = None\n    ) -> VerificationResponse:\n        """\n        Verify an operation using Aristotle\n        \n        Args:\n            operation: Operation type\n            content: Content to verify\n            context: Additional context\n            custom_criteria: Custom verification criteria\n        \n        Returns:\n            VerificationResponse object\n        """\n        from aristotle_client import AristotleClient\n        \n        # Get risk level\n        risk_level = self.get_risk_level(operation)\n        \n        # Generate verification criteria\n        if custom_criteria:\n            criteria = custom_criteria\n        else:\n            criteria = self._generate_criteria(operation, context)\n        \n        # Get Aristotle client\n        aristotle = None\n        try:\n            from llm_integration_manager import llm_manager,     \n        # Perform verification\n        start_time = datetime.now()\n        \n        try:\n            is_valid, confidence, explanation = await aristotle.verify(\n                content=content,\n                criteria=criteria,\n                max_tokens=1024\n            )\n            \n            verification_time = (datetime.now() - start_time).total_seconds()\n            \n            # Determine result based on confidence and validity\n            result = self._determine_result(is_valid, confidence, risk_level)\n            \n            # Log verification\n            self._log_verification(operation, result, confidence, explanation)\n            \n            return VerificationResponse(\n                result=result,\n                confidence=confidence,\n                explanation=explanation,\n                verified_by="aristotle",\n                verification_time=verification_time,\n                timestamp=datetime.now()\n            )\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Verification failed: {str(e)}")\n            \n            return VerificationResponse(\n                result=VerificationResult.REQUIRES_REVIEW,\n                confidence=0.0,\n                explanation=f"Verification error: {str(e)}",\n                verified_by="error",\n State transition is logical and valid\n2. Child states are properly structured\n3. Confidence levels are appropriate\n4. No circular dependencies introduced\n5. State evolution follows system rules\n""",\n            OperationType.STATE_ROLLBACK: """\nVerify state rollback operation:\n1. Rollback target is valid ancestor\n2. No critical data will be lost\n""",\n            OperationType.AGENT_ASSIGNMENT: """\nVerify agent assignment operation:\n1. Agent has required capabilities\n2. Assignment is appropriate for agent role\n3. No conflicting assignments\n4. Resource constraints respected\n5. Assignment aligns with system goals\n""",\n            OperationType.GATE_CREATION: """\nVerify gate creation operation:\n1. Gate criteria are clear and measurable\n2. Gate aligns with system architecture\n""",\n            OperationType.SWARM_EXECUTION: """\nVerify swarm execution operation:\n1. Swarm configuration is valid\n2. Expected outcomes are realistic\n""",\n            OperationType.DOCUMENT_GENERATION: """\nVerify document generation operation:\n1. Document structure is valid\n2. Content is appropriate for purpose\n3. No sensitive data included\n4. Formatting is consistent\n5. Document meets quality standards\n""",\n            OperationType.SYSTEM_INITIALIZATION: """\nVerify system initialization operation:\n1. Initialization parameters are valid\n2. Required resources are available\n3. Initialization sequence is correct\n4. No conflicts with existing state\n5. Initialization is idempotent\n"""\n        }\n        \n        return criteria_templates.get(operation, "Verify operation meets quality and safety standards.")\n    \n    def _determine_result(\n        self,\n        is_valid: bool,\n        confidence: float,\n        risk_level: RiskLevel\n    ) -> VerificationResult:\n        """Determine verification result"""\n        \n        # High confidence and valid\n        if is_valid and confidence >= self.auto_verify_threshold:\n            return VerificationResult.VERIFIED\n        \n        # Invalid or low confidence for high-risk operations\n        if not is_valid or confidence < self.medium_risk_threshold:\n            if risk_level in [RiskLevel.HIGH, RiskLevel.CRITICAL]:\n                return VerificationResult.REJECTED\n            else:\n                return VerificationResult.REQUIRES_REVIEW\n        \n        # Medium confidence\n        if confidence >= self.high_risk_threshold:\n            return VerificationResult.VERIFIED\n        elif confidence >= self.medium_risk_threshold:\n            return VerificationResult.REQUIRES_REVIEW\n        else:\n            return VerificationResult.REJECTED\n    \n    def _log_verification(\n        self,\n        operation: OperationType,\n        result: VerificationResult,\n        confidence: float,\n        explanation: str\n    ):\n        """Log verification for audit trail"""\n        log_entry = {\n            \'operation\': operation.value,\n            \'result\': result.value,\n            \'confidence\': confidence,\n            \'explanation\': explanation,\n            \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n        }\n        \n        self.verification_history.append(log_entry)\n        \n        # Keep only last 1000 entries\n        if len(self.verification_history) > 1000:\n            self.verification_history = self.verification_history[-1000:]\n        \n        logger.info(f"Verification logged: {operation.value} -> {result.value} ({confidence:.2f})")\n    \n    def get_verification_history(\n        self,\n        operation: Optional[OperationType] = None,\n        limit: int = 100\n    ) -> List[Dict]:\n        """\n        Get verification history\n        \n        Args:\n            operation: Filter by operation type\n            limit: Maximum number of entries\n        \n        Returns:\n            List of verification entries\n        """\n        history = self.verification_history\n        \n        if operation:\n statistics"""\n        total = len(self.verification_history)\n        \n        if total == 0:\n            return {\n                \'total_verifications\': 0,\n                \'verified_count\': 0,\n                \'rejected_count\': 0,\n                \'review_count\': 0,\n                \'average_confidence\': 0.0\n            }\n        \n        verified = sum(1 for e in self.verification_history if e[\'result\'] == \'verified\')\n        rejected = sum(1 for e in self.verification_history if e[\'result\'] == \'rejected\')\n        review = sum(1 for e in self.verification_history if e[\'result\'] == \'requires_review\')\n        \n        avg_confidence = sum(e[\'confidence\'] for e in self.verification_history) / total\n        \n        return {\n            \'total_verifications\': total,\n            \'verified_count\': verified,\n            \'rejected_count\': rejected,\n            \'review_count\': review,\n            \'average_confidence\': avg_confidence,\n            \'verification_rate\': verified / total if total > 0 else 0.0\n        }\n\n\n# Global verification system instance\nverification_system = {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '## Phase 4: Swarm Execution with Real LLMs\n\nNow let me implement the swarm execution system with parallel LLM calling.\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="swarm_execution_system.py">\n"""\nMurphy System - Phase 4: Swarm Execution with Real LLMs\nParallel LLM execution for swarm processing\n"""\n\nimport asyncio\nimport logging\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Tuple, Optional\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\nimport uuid\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\nclass SwarmType(Enum):\n    """Types of swarms"""\n    CREATIVE = "creative"\n    ANALYTICAL = "analytical"\n    HYBRID = "hybrid"\n    ADVERSARIAL = "adversarial"\n    SYNTHESIS = "synthesis"\n    OPTIMIZATION = "optimization"\n\n\nclass SwarmStatus(Enum):\n    """Swarm status"""\n    IDLE = "idle"\n    RUNNING = "running"\n    COMPLETED = "completed"\n    FAILED = "failed"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass SwarmAgent:\n    """Individual swarm agent"""\n    id: str\n    name: str\n    type: SwarmType\n    prompt: str\n    result: Optional[str] = None\n    confidence: float = 0.0\n    status: str = "pending"\n    tokens_used: int = 0\n    generation_time: float = 0.0\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass SwarmResult:\n    """Swarm execution result"""\n    swarm_id: str\n    agents: List[SwarmAgent]\n    synthesized_result: str\n    consensus_confidence: float\n    status: SwarmStatus\n    execution_time: float\n    timestamp: datetime\n\n\nclass SwarmExecutionSystem:\n    """Swarm execution system with parallel LLM processing"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        """Initialize swarm system"""\n        self.active_swarms: Dict[str, SwarmResult] = {}\n        self.swarm_history: List[SwarmResult] = []\n        self.max_parallel_agents = 6  # Limit concurrent LLM calls\n        \n        logger.info("Swarm Execution System initialized")\n    \n    async def execute_swarm(\n        self,\n        task: str,\n        swarm_type: SwarmType = SwarmType.HYBRID,\n        context: Dict = None,\n        num_agents: int = 3\n    ) -> SwarmResult:\n        """\n        Execute a swarm task with parallel LLM processing\n        \n        Args:\n            task: Task description\n            swarm_type: Type of swarm to execute\n            context: Additional context\n            num_agents: Number of agents in swarm\n        \n        Returns:\n            SwarmResult object\n        """\n        swarm_id = f"swarm_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}"\n        start_time = datetime.now()\n        \n        logger.info(f"Starting swarm {swarm_id} with {num_agents} agents")\n        \n        # Create swarm agents\n        agents = self._create_swarm_agents(task, swarm_type, context, num_agents, swarm_id)\n        \n        # Execute agents in parallel\n        try:\n            results = await self._execute_agents_parallel(agents)\n            \n            # Synthesize results\n            synthesized_result, consensus = await self._synthesize_results(\n                results, swarm_type, task\n            )\n            \n            # Create swarm result\n            swarm_result = SwarmResult(\n                swarm_id=swarm_id,\n                agents=results,\n                synthesized_result=synthesized_result,\n                consensus_confidence=consensus,\n                status=SwarmStatus.COMPLETED,\n                execution_time=(datetime.now() - start_time).total_seconds(),\n                timestamp=datetime.now()\n            )\n            \n            # Store result\n            self.active_swarms[swarm_id] = swarm_result\n            self.swarm_history.append(swarm_result)\n            \n            logger.info(f"Swarm {swarm_id} completed in {swarm_result.execution_time:.2f}s")\n            \n            return swarm_result\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Swarm {swarm_id} failed: {str(e)}")\n            \n            # Create failed result\n            swarm_result = SwarmResult(\n                swarm_id=swarm_id,\n                agents=agents,\n                synthesized_result=f"Swarm execution failed: {str(e)}",\n                consensus_confidence=0.0,\n                status=SwarmStatus.FAILED,\n                execution_time=(datetime.now() - start_time).total_seconds(),\n                timestamp=datetime.now()\n            )\n            \n            return swarm_result\n    \n    def _create_swarm_agents(\n        self,\n        task: str,\n        swarm_type: SwarmType,\n        context: Dict,\n        num_agents: int,\n        swarm_id: str\n    ) -> List[SwarmAgent]:\n        """Create swarm agents with type-specific prompts"""\n        agents = []\n        \n        # Type-specific prompt templates\n        prompt_templates = self._get_prompt_templates(swarm_type)\n        \n        for i in range(num_agents):\n            agent_id = f"{swarm_id}_agent_{i+1}"\n            \n            # Select prompt template\n            prompt_template = prompt_templates[i % len(prompt_templates)]\n            \n            # Format prompt with context\n            context_str = self._format_context(context) if context else ""\n            prompt = f"{prompt_template}\\n\\nTask: {task}\\n{context_str}"\n            \n            agent = SwarmAgent(\n                id=agent_id,\n                name=f"{swarm_type.value.capitalize()} Agent {i+1}",\n                type=swarm_type,\n                prompt=prompt,\n                status="pending"\n            )\n            \n            agents.append(agent)\n        \n        return agents\n    \n    def _get_prompt_templates(self, swarm_type: SwarmType) -> List[str]:\n        """Get prompt templates for swarm type"""\n        templates = {\n            SwarmType.CREATIVE: [\n                "Think creatively and explore diverse possibilities. Brainstorm innovative solutions without constraints.",\n                "Consider unconventional approaches and wild ideas. Think outside the box.",\n                "Focus on novelty and originality. Propose groundbreaking concepts."\n            ],\n            SwarmType.ANALYTICAL: [\n                "Analyze the problem systematically. Break it down into components and examine each thoroughly.",\n                "Use data-driven reasoning. Consider logical implications and dependencies.",\n                "Apply critical thinking. Identify assumptions and evaluate their validity."\n            ],\n            SwarmType.HYBRID: [\n                "Combine creative and analytical thinking. Balance innovation with practicality.",\n                "Consider both big-picture vision and detailed implementation.",\n                "Integrate diverse perspectives into a cohesive solution."\n            ],\n            SwarmType.ADVERSARIAL: [\n                "Challenge the assumptions and propose counter-arguments. Find weaknesses in proposed solutions.",\n                "Play devil\'s advocate. Identify potential failure modes and risks.",\n                "Question the premises and explore alternative viewpoints."\n            ],\n            SwarmType.SYNTHESIS: [\n                "Integrate multiple viewpoints into a unified solution. Find common ground.",\n                "Synthesize diverse ideas into a coherent whole. Balance competing requirements.",\n                "Create a harmonious solution that incorporates the best elements of each perspective."\n            ],\n            SwarmType.OPTIMIZATION: [\n                "Optimize for efficiency and performance. Minimize waste and maximize value.",\n                "Refine and improve the solution. Eliminate redundancies and streamline processes.",\n                "Focus on quality and effectiveness. Ensure the solution meets all requirements optimally."\n            ]\n        }\n        \n        return templates.get(swarm_type, ["Provide a thoughtful solution to the task."])\n    \n    def _format_context(self, context: Dict) -> str:\n        """Format context as string"""\n        lines = []\n        for key, value in context.items():\n            lines.append(f"{key}: {value}")\n        return "\\n".join(lines)\n    \n    async def _execute_agents_parallel(self, agents: List[SwarmAgent]) -> List[SwarmAgent]:\n        """Execute agents in parallel"""\n        from llm_integration_manager import llm_manager\n        \n        # Create tasks for each agent\n        tasks = []\n        for agent in agents:\n            task = self._execute_single_agent(agent, llm_manager)\n            tasks.append(task)\n        \n        # Execute all tasks in parallel\n        results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)\n        \n        # Process results\n        completed_agents = []\n        for agent, result in zip(agents, results):\n            if isinstance(result, Exception):\n                logger.error(f"Agent {agent.id} failed: {str(result)}")\n                agent.status = "failed"\n                agent.result = f"Error: {str(result)}"\n            else:\n                agent.status = "completed"\n                agent.result = result[\'content\']\n                agent.confidence = result[\'confidence\']\n                agent.tokens_used = result[\'tokens_used\']\n                agent.generation_time = result[\'generation_time\']\n            \n            completed_agents.append(agent)\n        \n        return completed_agents\n    \n    async def _execute_single_agent(\n        self,\n        agent: SwarmAgent,\n        llm_manager\n    ) -> Dict:\n        """Execute a single agent"""\n        agent.status = "running"\n        \n        try:\n            response = await llm_manager.call_llm(\n                prompt=agent.prompt,\n                max_tokens=1024,\n                use_cache=False  # Always generate fresh for swarms\n            )\n            \n            return {\n                \'content\': response.content,\n                \'confidence\': response.confidence,\n                \'tokens_used\': response.tokens_used,\n                \'generation_time\': response.generation_time\n            }\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Agent execution error: {str(e)}")\n            raise\n    \n    async def _synthesize_results(\n        self,\n        agents: List[SwarmAgent],\n        swarm_type: SwarmType,\n        original_task: str\n    ) -> Tuple[str, float]:\n        """Synthesize results from multiple agents"""\n        from llm_integration_manager import llm_manager\n        \n        # Filter out failed agents\n        successful_agents = [a for a in agents if a.status == "completed"]\n        \n        if not successful_agents:\n            return "No successful agent results", 0.0\n        \n        # Build synthesis prompt\n        agent_results = "\\n\\n".join([\n            f"Agent {i+1} ({a.name}):\\n{a.result}"\n            for i, a in enumerate(successful_agents)\n        ])\n        \n        synthesis_prompt = f"""Synthesize the following swarm agent results into a cohesive response.\n\nOriginal Task: {original_task}\nSwarm Type: {swarm_type.value}\n\nAgent Results:\n{agent_results}\n\nProvide:\n1. A unified, synthesized response\n2. Key insights from each agent\n3. Consensus or conflicting viewpoints\n4. Final recommendation or conclusion\n\nFormat as a clear, professional synthesis."""\n        \n        # Synthesize using LLM\n        try:\n            response = await llm_manager.call_llm(\n                prompt=synthesis_prompt,\n                max_tokens=1536,\n                use_cache=False\n            )\n            \n            # Calculate consensus confidence\n            confidences = [a.confidence for a in successful_agents]\n            consensus = sum(confidences) / len(confidences)\n            \n            return response.content, consensus\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Synthesis failed: {str(e)}")\n            \n            # Fallback: return best agent result\n            best_agent = max(successful_agents, key=lambda a: a.confidence)\n            return best_agent.result, best_agent.confidence\n    \n    def get_active_swarms(self) -> List[SwarmResult]:\n        """Get all active swarms"""\n        return list(self.active_swarms.values())\n    \n    def get_swarm_history(self, limit: int = 50) -> List[SwarmResult]:\n        """Get swarm execution history"""\n        return self.swarm_history[-limit:]\n    \n    def get_swarm(self, swarm_id: str) -> Optional[SwarmResult]:\n        """Get specific swarm result"""\n        return self.active_swarms.get(swarm_id)\n\n\n# Global swarm system instance\nswarm_system = SwarmExecutionSystem()\n\n\nasync def test_swarm_system():\n    """Test swarm execution system"""\n    print("\\n" + "="*60)\n    print("SWARM EXECUTION SYSTEM TEST")\n    print("="*60)\n    \n    #       # > 0.50\n    VERY_LOW = "very_low"      # <= 0.50\n\n\nclass ExecutionPolicy(Enum):\n    """Execution policies based on confidence"""\n    AUTO_EXECUTE = "auto_execute"       # Very high \n        Args:\n            operation: Operation type\n            content: Operation content\n            llm_response: LLM response if available\n            verification_result: Verification factors[\'llm_quality\'] = self._assess_llm_quality(llm_response)\n        else:\n            factors[\'llm_quality\'] = 0.5  # Neutral if no LLM\n        \n        # Factor 3: Verification confidence (0-0.3)\n        if verification_result:\n            factors[\'verification\'] = verification_result.get(\'confidence\', 0.5)\n        else:\n            factors[\'verification\'] = 0.5  # Neutral if        factors[\'context_relevance\'] = 0.5\n        \n        # Calculate weighted average\n        weights = {\n            \'content_quality\': 0.3,\n            \'llm_quality\': 0.3,\n            \'verification\': 0.3,\n            \'context_relevance\': 0.1\n        }\n        \n        confidence = sum(\n            factors[factor] * weight\n            for factor, weight in     \n        # Length factor\n        length = len(content)\n        if length >= 100:\n            score += 0.2\n        elif length >= 50:\n            score += 0.1\n        \n        # Structure factor\n        if \'\\n\' in content:\n            score += 0.1\n        if any(marker in content for marker in [\'•\', \'-\', \'1.\', \'2.\', \'3.\']):\n            score += 0.1\n        \n        # Coherence factor (simple check)\n        sentences = content.split(\'.\')\n        meaningful_sentences = [s for s in sentences if len(s.strip()) > 10]\n        if len(meaningful_sentences) >= 2:\n            score += 0.1\n        \n        return min(score, 1.0)\n    \n    def _assess_llm_quality(self, response: str) -> float:\n        """Assess LLM response quality (0-1)"""\n        if not response:\n            return 0.0\n        \n        score = 0.5\n        \n        # Length\n        if len(response) >= 200:\n            score += 0.2\n        elif len(response) >= 100:\n \n        # Specific context types\n        if any(key in context for key in [\'recent_commands\', \'goals\', \'preferences\']):\n            score += 0.2\n        \n        return min(score, 1.0)\n    \n    def _get_confidence_level(self, confidence: float) -> ConfidenceLevel:\n        """Get confidence level from score"""\n        if confidence >= 0.95:\n            return \').title()\n            explanation_parts.append(f"{factor_display}: {value:.2f}")\n        \n        # Add overall\n        explanation_parts.append(f"Overall confidence: {confidence:.2f}")\n        \n        return " | ".join(explanation_parts)\n    \n    def make_execution_decision(\n        self,\n        confidence: ConfidenceScore,\n        risk_level: str = "medium"\n    ) ->
